4526 
4527 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
4528 #define CHARSET_NAME        "CP932//"
4529 #define FROM_LOOP       from_cp932
4530 #define TO_LOOP         to_cp932
4531 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
4532 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
4533 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
4534 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     2
4535 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       4
4536 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0
4537 
4538 /* First define the conversion function from CP932 to UCS4.  */
4539 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4540 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4541 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
4542 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
4543 #define BODY \
4544   {                                       \
4545     uint32_t ch = *inptr;                             \
4546                                           \
4547     if (ch < 0x80)                                \
4548       ++inptr;                                    \
4549     else if (ch >= 0xa1 && ch <= 0xdf)                                        \
4550       {                                                                       \
4551     ch += 0xfec0;                                                         \
4552     ++inptr;                                                              \
4553       }                                       \
4554     else if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == 0xa0                     \
4555          || __builtin_expect (ch <= 0x80, 0)                  \
4556          || __builtin_expect (ch > 0xfc, 0))                  \
4557       {                                       \
4558     /* These are illegal.  */                         \
4559     if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4560       {                                   \
4561         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4562         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4563         break;                                \
4564       }                                   \
4565                                           \
4566     ++inptr;                                  \
4567     ++*irreversible;                              \
4568     continue;                                 \
4569       }                                       \
4570     else                                      \
4571       {                                       \
4572     /* Two-byte character.  First test whether the next character         \
4573        is also available.  */                         \
4574     uint32_t ch2;                                 \
4575     uint_fast32_t idx;                            \
4576                                           \
4577     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
4578       {                                   \
4579         /* The second character is not available.  Store              \
4580            the intermediate result.  */                   \
4581         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
4582         break;                                \
4583       }                                   \
4584                                           \
4585     ch2 = inptr[1];                               \
4586     idx = ch * 256 + ch2;                             \
4587     if (__builtin_expect (ch2 < 0x40, 0)                      \
4588         || __builtin_expect (ch2 > 0xfc, 0)                   \
4589         || __builtin_expect (ch2 == 0x7f, 0)                  \
4590         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x84be, 0) && idx < 0x8740)       \
4591         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x879c, 0) && idx < 0x889f)       \
4592         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x88fc, 0) && idx < 0x8940)       \
4593         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0x9ffc, 0) && idx < 0xe040)       \
4594         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0xeaa4, 0) && idx < 0xed40)       \
4595         || (__builtin_expect (idx > 0xeefc, 0) && idx < 0xf040)       \
4596         || __builtin_expect (idx > 0xfc4b, 0))                \
4597       {                                   \
4598         /* This is illegal.  */                       \
4599         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4600           {                                   \
4601         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4602         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4603         break;                                \
4604           }                                   \
4605                                           \
4606         ++inptr;                                  \
4607         ++*irreversible;                              \
4608         continue;                                 \
4609       }                                   \
4610                                           \
4611     /* We could pack the data a bit more dense.  The second           \
4612        byte will never be 0x7f and it will also be never              \
4613        >0xfc.  But this would mean yet more `if's.  */            \
4614     if (idx <= 0x84be)                            \
4615       ch = cjk_block1[(ch - 0x81) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4616     else if (idx <= 0x879c)                           \
4617       ch = cjk_block2[(ch - 0x87) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4618     else if (idx <= 0x88fc)                           \
4619       ch = cjk_block3[(ch - 0x88) * 192 + ch2 - 0x9f];            \
4620     else if (idx <= 0x9ffc)                           \
4621       ch = cjk_block4[(ch - 0x89) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4622     else if (idx <= 0xeaa4)                           \
4623       ch = cjk_block5[(ch - 0xe0) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4624     else if (idx <= 0xeefc)                           \
4625       ch = cjk_block6[(ch - 0xed) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4626     else if (idx <= 0xf9fc)                           \
4627       ch = (ch-0xf0)*188 + ch2-((ch2<0x7f)?0x40:0x41) + 0xe000;       \
4628     else                                      \
4629       ch = cjk_block7[(ch - 0xfa) * 192 + ch2 - 0x40];            \
4630                                           \
4631     if (__builtin_expect (ch, 1) == 0)                    \
4632       {                                   \
4633         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4634         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4635           {                                   \
4636         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4637         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4638         break;                                \
4639           }                                   \
4640                                           \
4641         inptr += 2;                               \
4642         ++*irreversible;                              \
4643         continue;                                 \
4644       }                                   \
4645                                           \
4646     inptr += 2;                               \
4647       }                                       \
4648                                           \
4649     put32 (outptr, ch);                               \
4650     outptr += 4;                                  \
4651   }
4652 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4653 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4654 
4655 
4656 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
4657 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
4658 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4659 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4660 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
4661 #define BODY \
4662   {                                       \
4663     uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr);                          \
4664     const char *cp;                               \
4665     unsigned char pua[2];                             \
4666                                           \
4667     if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0])))         \
4668       {                                       \
4669     if (ch >= 0x0391 && ch <= 0x0451)                     \
4670       cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x391];                   \
4671     else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa0)                    \
4672       cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x2010];                    \
4673     else if (ch >= 0xe000 && ch <= 0xe757)                    \
4674       {                                   \
4675         pua[0] = (ch - 0xe000) / 188 + 0xf0;                  \
4676         pua[1] = (ch - 0xe000) % 188 + 0x40;                  \
4677         if (pua[1] > 0x7e)                            \
4678           pua[1]++;                               \
4679         cp = (const char *)&(pua[0]);                     \
4680       }                                   \
4681     else if (ch >= 0xf929 && ch <= 0xfa2d)                    \
4682       cp = from_ucs4_cjkcpt[ch - 0xf929];                     \
4683     else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1)               \
4684          && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffe5, 1))               \
4685       cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff01];                      \
4686     else                                      \
4687       {                                   \
4688         UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4);                      \
4689         /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4690         cp = "";                                  \
4691       }                                   \
4692       }                                       \
4693     else                                      \
4694       cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch];                            \
4695                                           \
4696     if (__builtin_expect (cp[0], '\1') == '\0' && ch != 0)            \
4697       {                                       \
4698     /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4699     STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
4700       }                                       \
4701     else                                      \
4702       {                                       \
4703     *outptr = cp[0];                              \
4704     /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible.  */\
4705     if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
4706       {                                   \
4707         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend))              \
4708           {                                   \
4709         /* The result does not fit into the buffer.  */           \
4710         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4711         break;                                \
4712           }                                   \
4713         *++outptr = cp[1];                            \
4714       }                                   \
4715     ++outptr;                                 \
4716       }                                       \
4717                                           \
4718     inptr += 4;                                   \
4719   }
4720 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4721 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4722 
4723 
4724 /* Now define the toplevel functions.  */
4725 #include <iconv/skeleton.c>
/* [<][>][^][v][top][bottom][index][help] */
